### Post by ajgreeny on 2014-10-23
You probably just need to make changes to the settings in Pulse Volume Control which you can get to from Sound Settings on the Volume icon in your panel (or from dash if using unity).

---

> **ajgreeny said:**

But I  don't know enough about Ubuntu or Alsa to do this.  As you will see there is a number of sound options on the screenshot (tried them all) including Analog Output and Speakers HDA Creative as I have Sound Blaster card.  Any further thoughts?

### Post by Douglas_H_Campbell on 2014-12-02
Bug 87771 - No sound in Linux after rebooting from Windows. Gigabyte GA-Z97-D3H motherboard. 

Status: 
RESOLVED CODE_FIX 

  [U][SIZE=3]Here's the fix which I am trying to understand and apply.[/SIZE]
[/U]
OK, then try to install hda-verb program (included in the latest alsa-tools package), and run like below as root on the non-working system:

    hda-verb /dev/snd/hwC0D2 0x20 SET_COEF_INDEX 0x07
    hda-verb /dev/snd/hwC0D2 0x20 SET_PROC_COEF 0x7cb0

**ANSWER**

root@meklon-desktop:/home/meklon# hda-verb /dev/snd/hwC0D2 0x20 SET_COEF_INDEX 0x07
nid = 0x20, verb = 0x500, param = 0x7
value = 0x0
root@meklon-desktop:/home/meklon# hda-verb /dev/snd/hwC0D2 0x20 SET_PROC_COEF 0x7cb0
nid = 0x20, verb = 0x400, param = 0x7cb0
value = 0x0

Some kind of black magic for me) Sound appears after this.

**REPLY**
Thank you for your attention. The bug is not critical. The can be a workaround with adding the script during the system startup.
hda-verb /dev/snd/hwC0D2 0x20 SET_COEF_INDEX 0x07
hda-verb /dev/snd/hwC0D2 0x20 SET_PROC_COEF 0x7cb0

---
